name:C‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçr‚Äço‚Äçy
info:Standard Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Booked for others
info:6 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted March 2, 2024
msg:Given the high rating and reputation of this hotel, I was shocked by the conditions of the supposedly newly renovated rooms.  I was staying at the standard room on the twelve floor , facing the historical buildings.  We checked in after 10:30pm under the drizzles and chill -  the outside temperature was around 10 degress.

I noticed the holes of the linen of the blinds when they were rolled down, though it could still function.  Yet, the light shield was worse.  It was trapped on one side and could not be let down.  

The plus side was we were offered another room on the same floor immediately.  Leo who helped to bring our luggage up was very polite and patient. He stayed outside our room when his colleague brought the new key of the new room and accompanied us to the new room to ensure everything was all right.  He was worth 5 out of 5 for service.  However, I would further explain why I only gave 4 out of 5 for service. 

Yet,  the new room was smaller and for any other international hotels , from my experience, would offer an upgrade of the room.  This hotel did not.  Thats why I gave 4 out of 5 for service.

The linen of the blinds in the new room was still far from 100%.  I could still detect torn tissues , most probably because the blinds were dated.  Thats why I gave a 3 out of 5 for facilities.
----------------------------------------

The hardware facilities are complete. The double sink design is easy to use. The bedding is also made of high yarn, so you can have a comfortable sleep when you are tired from playing.
‚ñ™Ô∏èThe hotel has two doors. The east door is the main entrance. It is located on the second floor and is also where the hotel lobby is. There is an exclusive road leading up from the People's Bridge. The north door opens on the sand surface side. There is a sign at the door. The "White Swan" where many people come here to check in and take photos, and there is also the famous Saqima store [Gourmet House] at the north gate.
‚ñ™Ô∏èAn exclusive advantage of staying at the White Swan is that you can book the popular two-story Michelin-starred [Hongtu Mansion] and the third-floor Black Pearl [Yujiang Chunnuan] in advance, saving you the trouble of queuing up to get a reservation, even if you want to go there at last minute When dining, you can also go to the front desk of the restaurant to get your guest number and be seated first.
‚ñ™Ô∏èIn short, staying at White Swan is a five-star experience. I am very satisfied. I will still choose this hotel next time I come to Guangzhou.

msg:I am a person who suffers from hotel selection syndrome, so I have to evaluate it carefully and objectively! I wrote this review while sleeping in bed at two or three in the morning before I checked out of the hotel. I will post it later after I review it. There are good experiences and there are very bad ones. As the first five-star hotel in China, it has hosted many national leaders. It is said that the morning tea ceiling is here, so I came here because of its reputation. The geographical location is excellent, within walking distance to Shamian, Shangxiajiu Pedestrian Street and Yongqingfang. The deluxe river view room is large in size and has a beautiful river view during the day. There is almost no night view at night and the lighting is very bleak. The service attitudes of the front desk and security are very good (except Hongtu Mansion, which will be discussed in detail later). Switching from an elegant hotel with almost perfect experience, once you enter the lobby, it is indeed overcrowded because non-resident guests can enter. This is understandable. After all, there are several major gourmet restaurants inside, and the public area inside the hotel is very beautiful. Let‚Äôs talk about the two well-known signature restaurants [Hongtufu] and [Yutang Chunnuan] in detail: [Hongtufu] morning tea is open from 8:00 to 14:30. I arrived at 13:30 and was still in line for table 21 because I was staying at the hotel. Guests were seated in two minutes. The large hall was indeed full. I ordered shrimp dumplings, chicken feet, swan cakes, Shaqima, Tingzai porridge, and palace Pu'er tea. In terms of taste, Shaqima was worthy of its reputation; shrimp dumplings and There is no difference between the ones at Guangzhou Restaurant; the Tingzi porridge is just average; the swan cake is almost a must because it looks good and tastes good; the chicken feet basically meet expectations; the palace Pu'er tea is delicious. In terms of service: Very average, especially the tea makers. They help the guests make the soup and then pour the tea into the male cups, and then the guests pour the tea into the small cups themselves. Every time they add tea, I say thank you, but they don‚Äôt. Upon hearing any response, you can feel their numb expressions wearing masks. I have to pay 15% of the consumption as service fee (requirement), that‚Äôs it? At 20:15, I wasn‚Äôt hungry at all, so I went to check in at [Yutang Chunnuan]. The environment was good, there was a pretty pond inside, koi were fed and surrounded by flowers and plants. I only ordered braised squab and white braised goose palm wings. The squab was delicious, and the goose wings were good at first. The more you ate, the more it tasted like pickled pepper and chicken feet, and it was a bit salty. The overall attitude of the waiters is better than that of Hongtufu. There is a guzheng player with decent skills. The hotel is located within the flight coverage area, and the aircraft noise is obvious before 12 pm. At 3 am, the sound of gray aircraft piercing the night sky was actually heard. In addition, I live on the 16th floor. Before 12 o'clock in the evening, I could hear noisy chatter coming from the guest rooms or public areas below. The guests on the upper floor of my room were unwilling to take off their high heels even after 12 o'clock. He seems to be taking a walk in the room, and I don‚Äôt know if he ate too much. Let me talk about my worst experience, the sleeping experience: due to work reasons, I changed my flight to a very early flight and returned early. I usually go to bed late, so I went to bed at 0:10. At 2:10, I woke up from a nigh**are and finally woke up. Come here, let‚Äôs analyze the possibilities in several aspects. First, before booking the hotel, we noticed that the bed was placed in an unusual direction. It was placed facing the river, that is, facing the window. This is equivalent to having your feet facing the window when sleeping. In short, if you are taboo about this, don‚Äôt book a room with river view. Secondly, it is possible that you may not be able to sleep well if you eat too much before going to bed. Third, the air conditioner may be old and therefore noisy. Fourth, the temperature is difficult to control, the bedding seems not very breathable, my head and hands are exposed and I feel cold, my body is stuffy and sweaty in the quilt, and the pillow is uncomfortable. So I only slept for two hours and I didn't dare to sleep after I was woken up by a nigh**are. Hey, I had a good night's sleep at Yazhi last night, and I slept for 7.5 hours. msg:On the last day of my stay in Guangzhou, I chose the White Swan Hotel. In summary, it is highly recommended, especially for couples, friends, and young people like me traveling.
I only considered White Swan because I was visiting Liwan. Before I checked in, I was always worried about the outdated facilities and poor experience, but it was actually completely ok.
Overall: Compared with the magnificent and oriental culture, I think White Swan has really achieved Chinese aesthetics and cultural heritage. The entire hotel has a layout of Lingnan landscape gardens as soon as you enter the door. There are three floors up and down the lobby. Check-in is on the second floor. The third floor is mainly a restaurant. It has the feel of a resort hotel. The door on the first floor is Shamian Island, and the location is invincible.
The sandalwood tones, humanistic picture books, and paintings that can be seen everywhere in the guest rooms all make people feel the hotel's intentions in the layout. The view is wide, and the whole room is bright and a**ospheric. The toilet is also an automatic toilet. In contrast, the brand of hair dryer and toiletries is a bit broken, and it is really not like a five-star hotel.
Meals: The hotel has Hongtufu, the number one morning tea restaurant in Guangzhou. We ordered takeaways to take back to the room to eat, avoiding long queues. For dinner, I chose Jin Yu Man Tang on the third floor, and went to Yu Nian Hua to drink cocktails and watch performances. The food part may have really raised the expectations too high, but I think it‚Äôs okay, the char siew buns are not bad, and there is nothing particularly amazing about the others. The bar recommends the Hawthorn Water Love Cocktail, which is delicious.
Service: Compared with the hotel environment, the service is really average. Chris in the lobby is very nice. He should be the manager of the lobby or the person in charge of the concierge depar**ent. He has customers in his eyes, and he will ask when he sees the wait, and his attitude is serious and responsible.
The check-in speed is extremely slow, there are obviously not many people, but the queue is almost 20 minutes. What I am most dissatisfied with this time is the restaurant service of Jinyu Mantang, which is basically equivalent to no service. I don‚Äôt understand what the service fee is for. I feel that the management still needs to strengthen the basic training.
Although the service is mediocre, the flaws are not hidden, and I can fully feel the culture of Guangzhou after living here for just two days. Next time I have a chance, I will bring my parents to play again!

msg:All great achievements are the result of continuous struggle; all great undertakings need to be advanced in the process of continuing the past and opening up the future.
üåüüåüüåüüåüüåüüåüüåüüåüüåüüåüüåüüåüüåüüåüüåüüåüüåü

White Swan Hotel is located in White Swan Pond, Shamian, Guangzhou City, Guangdong Province. It was invested and constructed by Mr. Huo Yingdong and the People's Government of Guangdong Province. It was jointly designed by the famous Chinese architectural design masters She Fannan and Mo Bozhi. China's first Sino-foreign cooperative five-star hotel.

üöñTransportation:
The hotel is located in Shamian Bai Swan Pond, which is said to be reclaimed from the sea. It is an independent building with very convenient transportation.

üè†Facilities:
The facilities of the White Swan Hotel are really good. The lobby is not too big, but there is an Internet celebrity spot `Hometown Water`, and a lot of tourists, diners and overseas Chinese come to punch in and take pictures every day.
This time, I stayed in the Executive Deluxe River View Twin Room, 60 square meters. As soon as I entered the door, there was a large walk-in corridor, with the wardrobe on the left and the washing area on the right. Walking in again is the room, which is very large and has a good structure. There are two windows on the left and right to see the river view. Three-person sofa, round dining table, long desk (with stationery in the drawer) everything.
The wash area has double washbasins, a single bathtub, the toilet and the shower room are separated, and the dry and wet are separated. Toiletries are ETRO in Italy.
The bedding is very comfortable, there are many choices of pillows, and the sleep is very good.
The gym and swimming pool of the hotel are in the back garden of the hotel. The gym is very large, with complete facilities and equipment; the swimming pool is outdoor and has a constant temperature. There is also a massage pool next to the swimming pool, which is also constant temperature. There are also dry steam and wet steam in the locker room, which is very good.

üõéÔ∏èService:
very good! Early contact, check-in, room service, cleaning, turndown, check-out and various communications were very smooth and comfortable. Thank you Mr. Huang Zhong, the assistant manager of the lobby, for his thoughtful arrangements and care!

üç≤ Catering:
I have been to Yutang Chunnuan of White Swan and Hongtu Mansion before. This time I went to the executive lounge of White Swan. As soon as you enter the lounge, you will see a large area of books, with all kinds of books, you can take them back to the room to read if you like. The lounge is decorated in Chinese style, low-key and luxurious. It is the most tasteful executive lounge I have ever been to. There are high bar chairs and low sofas, which are very comfortable. There is also a small meeting room that can accommodate a dozen people. There is a long row of floor-to-ceiling glass windows by the window of the lounge, and the scenery of the sand surface is unobstructed.
There are six kinds of foreign wines in the lounge, which are very rich and can be adjusted to various cocktails. The food variety is not much, but it is exquisite. Afternoon tea, happy hour, buffet breakfast are all satisfied, and the service is very good! The waiter Xiaoye (a handsome little brother) is always smiling, and can quickly and accurately get the needs of the guests, which is very warm [happy]
